I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[Bug]: NVIDIADriver CRs remain stuck after deleting conflicting default CR due to missing requeue of peer NVIDIADriver resources
_**Important Note:  NVIDIA AI Enterprise customers can get support from NVIDIA Enterprise support. Please open a case [here](https://enterprise-support.nvidia.com/s/create-case)**._

**Describe the bug**
When multiple NVIDIADriver CRs are present, conflict validation is evaluated globally across all CR node selectors. If the default NVIDIADriver (no explicit selector) overlaps with custom CRs, custom CRs fail validation and exit reconcile without requeue.
After deleting the default/conflicting CR, the previously blocked CRs do not automatically reconcile, so they remain stuck until a separate unrelated event triggers them.

**To Reproduce**
Deploy GPU Operator with default NVIDIADriver CR.
Create 2+ custom NVIDIADriver CRs with unique [nodeSelector](vscode-file://vscode-app/Applications/Visual%20Studio%20Code.app/Contents/Resources/app/out/vs/code/electron-browser/workbench/workbench.html) labels.
Label nodes to match custom CR selectors.
Observe custom CRs are blocked due to conflict with default CR.
Delete the default NVIDIADriver CR.
Observe blocked custom CRs do not progress automatically.

**Expected behavior**
Deleting/updating a NVIDIADriver CR that changes global conflict state should trigger reconciliation of other NVIDIADriver CRs so they revalidate and proceed.

**Environment (please provide the following information):**
 - GPU Operator Version: v26.3.0
 - OS: ubuntu24.04, ubuntu22.04
 - Kubernetes Distro and Version: kubeadm 1.34

Collecting full debug bundle (optional):

```
curl -o must-gather.sh -L https://raw.githubusercontent.com/NVIDIA/gpu-operator/main/hack/must-gather.sh
chmod +x must-gather.sh
./must-gather.sh
```
**NOTE**: please refer to the [must-gather](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/NVIDIA/gpu-operator/main/hack/must-gather.sh) script for debug data collected.

This bundle can be submitted to us via email: **operator_feedback@nvidia.com**


</pr_description>

    52	// NVIDIADriverReconciler reconciles a NVIDIADriver object
    53	type NVIDIADriverReconciler struct {
    54	        client.Client
    55	        Scheme      *runtime.Scheme
    56	        ClusterInfo clusterinfo.Interface
    57	        Namespace   string
    58	
    59	        stateManager          state.Manager
    60	        nodeSelectorValidator validator.Validator
    61	        conditionUpdater      conditions.Updater
    62	}
    63	
    64	//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=nvidia.com,resources=nvidiadrivers,verbs=get;list;watch;create;update;patch;delete
    65	//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=nvidia.com,resources=nvidiadrivers/status,verbs=get;update;patch
    66	//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=nvidia.com,resources=nvidiadrivers/finalizers,verbs=update
    67	
    68	// Reconcile is part of the main kubernetes reconciliation loop which aims to
    69	// move the current state of the cluster closer to the desired state.
    70	// TODO(user): Modify the Reconcile function to compare the state specified by
    71	// the NVIDIADriver object against the actual cluster state, and then
    72	// perform operations to make the cluster state reflect the state specified by
    73	// the user.
    74	//
    75	// For more details, check Reconcile and its Result here:
    76	// - https://pkg.go.dev/sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime@v0.8.3/pkg/reconcile
    77	func (r *NVIDIADriverReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
    78	        logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
    79	        logger.V(consts.LogLevelInfo).Info("Reconciling NVIDIADriver")
    80	
    81	        // Get the NvidiaDriver instance from this request
    82	        instance := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{}
    83	        if err := r.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, instance); err != nil {
    84	                if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
    85	                        // Request object not found, could have been deleted after reconcile request.
    86	                        // Owned objects are automatically garbage collected. For additional cleanup logic use finalizers.
    87	                        // Return and don't requeue
    88	                        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
    89	                }
    90	                wrappedErr := fmt.Errorf("error getting NVIDIADriver object: %w", err)
    91	                logger.Error(err, "error getting NVIDIADriver object")
    92	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
    93	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, wrappedErr.Error()); condErr != nil {
    94	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
    95	                }
    96	                // Error reading the object - requeue the request.
    97	                return reconcile.Result{}, wrappedErr
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        // Get the singleton NVIDIA ClusterPolicy object in the cluster.
   101	        clusterPolicyList := &gpuv1.ClusterPolicyList{}
   102	        if err := r.List(ctx, clusterPolicyList); err != nil {
   103	                wrappedErr := fmt.Errorf("error getting ClusterPolicy list: %w", err)
   104	                logger.Error(err, "error getting ClusterPolicy list")
   105	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   106	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   107	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   108	                }
   109	                return reconcile.Result{}, wrappedErr
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        if len(clusterPolicyList.Items) == 0 {
   113	                err := fmt.Errorf("no ClusterPolicy object found in the cluster")
   114	                logger.Error(err, "failed to get ClusterPolicy object")
   115	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   116	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   117	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   118	                }
   119	                return reconcile.Result{}, err
   120	        }
   121	        clusterPolicyInstance := clusterPolicyList.Items[0]
   122	
   123	        // Ensure that ClusterPolicy is configured to use NVIDIADriver CRD
   124	        if !clusterPolicyInstance.Spec.Driver.UseNvidiaDriverCRDType() {
   125	                msg := "useNvidiaDriverCRD is not enabled in ClusterPolicy"
   126	                logger.V(consts.LogLevelWarning).Info("NVIDIADriver reconciliation skipped", "reason", msg)
   127	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.Disabled
   128	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.Reconciled, msg); condErr != nil {
   129	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   130	                }
   131	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        // Create a new InfoCatalog which is a generic interface for passing information to state managers
   135	        infoCatalog := state.NewInfoCatalog()
   136	
   137	        // Add an entry for ClusterInfo, which was collected before the NVIDIADriver controller was started
   138	        infoCatalog.Add(state.InfoTypeClusterInfo, r.ClusterInfo)
   139	
   140	        // Add an entry for Clusterpolicy, which is needed to deploy the driver daemonset
   141	        infoCatalog.Add(state.InfoTypeClusterPolicyCR, clusterPolicyInstance)
   142	
   143	        // Verify the nodeSelector configured for this NVIDIADriver instance does
   144	        // not conflict with any other instances. This ensures only one driver
   145	        // is deployed per GPU node.
   146	        if err := r.nodeSelectorValidator.Validate(ctx, instance); err != nil {
   147	                logger.Error(err, "nodeSelector validation failed")
   148	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   149	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ConflictingNodeSelector, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   150	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   151	                }
   152	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        if instance.Spec.UsePrecompiledDrivers() && (instance.Spec.IsGDSEnabled() || instance.Spec.IsGDRCopyEnabled()) {
   156	                err := errors.New("GPUDirect Storage driver (nvidia-fs) and/or GDRCopy driver is not supported along with pre-compiled NVIDIA drivers")
   157	                logger.Error(err, "unsupported driver combination detected")
   158	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   159	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   160	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   161	                }
   162	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if instance.Spec.IsGDSEnabled() && instance.Spec.IsOpenKernelModulesRequired() && !instance.Spec.IsOpenKernelModulesEnabled() {
   166	                err := fmt.Errorf("GPUDirect Storage driver '%s' is only supported with NVIDIA OpenRM drivers. Please set 'useOpenKernelModules=true' to enable OpenRM mode", instance.Spec.GPUDirectStorage.Version)
   167	                logger.Error(err, "unsupported driver combination detected")
   168	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   169	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   170	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   171	                }
   172	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        // ensure that the specified K8s secret actually exists in the operator namespace
   176	        secretName := instance.Spec.SecretEnv
   177	        if len(secretName) > 0 {
   178	                key := client.ObjectKey{Namespace: r.Namespace, Name: secretName}
   179	                if err := r.Get(ctx, key, &corev1.Secret{}); err != nil {
   180	                        logger.Error(err, "failed to get secret")
   181	                        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   182	                                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   183	                        }
   184	                        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   185	                }
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        // Sync state and update status
   189	        managerStatus := r.stateManager.SyncState(ctx, instance, infoCatalog)
   190	
   191	        // update CR status
   192	        if err := r.updateCrStatus(ctx, instance, managerStatus); err != nil {
   193	                return ctrl.Result{}, err
   194	        }
   195	
   196	        if managerStatus.Status != state.SyncStateReady {
   197	                logger.Info("NVIDIADriver instance is not ready")
   198	                var errorInfo error
   199	                for _, result := range managerStatus.StatesStatus {
   200	                        if result.Status != state.SyncStateReady && result.ErrInfo != nil {
   201	                                errorInfo = result.ErrInfo
   202	                                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, fmt.Sprintf("Error syncing state %s: %v", result.StateName, errorInfo.Error())); condErr != nil {
   203	                                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   204	                                }
   205	                                break
   206	                        }
   207	                }
   208	                // if no errors are reported from any state, then we would be waiting on driver daemonset pods
   209	                if errorInfo == nil {
   210	                        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.DriverNotReady, "Waiting for driver pod to be ready"); condErr != nil {
   211	                                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   212	                        }
   213	                }
   214	                return reconcile.Result{RequeueAfter: time.Second * 5}, nil
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsReady(ctx, instance, conditions.Reconciled, "All resources have been successfully reconciled"); condErr != nil {
   218	                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   219	                return ctrl.Result{}, condErr
   220	        }
   221	        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   222	}
   223	
   224	func (r *NVIDIADriverReconciler) updateCrStatus(
   225	        ctx context.Context, cr *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver, status state.Results) error {
   226	        reqLogger := log.FromContext(ctx)
   227	
   228	        // Fetch latest instance and update state to avoid version mismatch
   229	        instance := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{}
   230	        err := r.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Name: cr.Name}, instance)
   231	        if err != nil {
   232	                reqLogger.Error(err, "Failed to get NVIDIADriver instance for status update")
   233	                return err
   234	        }
   235	
   236	        // Update global State
   237	        if instance.Status.State == nvidiav1alpha1.State(status.Status) {
   238	                return nil
   239	        }
   240	        instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.State(status.Status)
   241	
   242	        // send status update request to k8s API
   243	        reqLogger.V(consts.LogLevelInfo).Info("Updating CR Status", "Status", instance.Status)
   244	        err = r.Status().Update(ctx, instance)
   245	        if err != nil {
   246	                reqLogger.Error(err, "Failed to update CR status")
   247	                return err
   248	        }
   249	        return nil
   250	}
   251	
   252	// SetupWithManager sets up the controller with the Manager.
   253	func (r *NVIDIADriverReconciler) SetupWithManager(ctx context.Context, mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
   254	        // Create state manager
   255	        stateManager, err := state.NewManager(
   256	                nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverCRDName,
   257	                r.Namespace,
   258	                mgr.GetClient(),
   259	                mgr.GetScheme())
   260	        if err != nil {
   261	                return fmt.Errorf("error creating state manager: %v", err)
   262	        }
   263	        r.stateManager = stateManager
   264	
   265	        // initialize validators
   266	        r.nodeSelectorValidator = validator.NewNodeSelectorValidator(r.Client)
   267	
   268	        // initialize condition updater
   269	        r.conditionUpdater = conditions.NewNvDriverUpdater(mgr.GetClient())
   270	
   271	        // Create a new NVIDIADriver controller
   272	        c, err := controller.New("nvidia-driver-controller", mgr, controller.Options{
   273	                Reconciler:              r,
   274	                MaxConcurrentReconciles: 1,
   275	                RateLimiter:             workqueue.NewTypedItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter[reconcile.Request](minDelayCR, maxDelayCR),
   276	        })
   277	        if err != nil {
   278	                return err
   279	        }
   280	
   281	        // Watch for changes to the primary resource NVIDIaDriver
   282	        err = c.Watch(source.Kind(
   283	                mgr.GetCache(),
   284	                &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{},
   285	                &handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{},
   286	                predicate.TypedGenerationChangedPredicate[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{},
   287	        ),
   288	        )
   289	        if err != nil {
   290	                return err
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        // Watch for changes to ClusterPolicy. Whenever an event is generated for ClusterPolicy, enqueue
   294	        // a reconcile request for all NVIDIADriver instances.
   295	        mapFn := func(ctx context.Context, cp *gpuv1.ClusterPolicy) []reconcile.Request {
   296	                logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
   297	                opts := []client.ListOption{}
   298	                list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}
   299	
   300	                err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
   301	                if err != nil {
   302	                        logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
   303	                        return []reconcile.Request{}
   304	                }
   305	
   306	                reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
   307	                for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
   308	                        reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
   309	                                reconcile.Request{
   310	                                        NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
   311	                                                Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
   312	                                                Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
   313	                                        },
   314	                                })
   315	                }
   316	
   317	                return reconcileRequests
   318	        }
   319	
   320	        // Watch for changes to the Nodes. Whenever an event is generated for ClusterPolicy, enqueue
   321	        // a reconcile request for all NVIDIADriver instances.
   322	        nodeMapFn := func(ctx context.Context, cp *corev1.Node) []reconcile.Request {
   323	                logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
   324	                opts := []client.ListOption{}
   325	                list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}
   326	
   327	                err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
   328	                if err != nil {
   329	                        logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
   330	                        return []reconcile.Request{}
   331	                }
   332	
   333	                reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
   334	                for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
   335	                        reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
   336	                                reconcile.Request{
   337	                                        NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
   338	                                                Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
   339	                                                Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
   340	                                        },
   341	                                })
   342	                }
   343	
   344	                return reconcileRequests
   345	        }
   346	
   347	        err = c.Watch(
   348	                source.Kind(
   349	                        mgr.GetCache(),
   350	                        &gpuv1.ClusterPolicy{},
   351	                        handler.TypedEnqueueRequestsFromMapFunc[*gpuv1.ClusterPolicy](mapFn),
   352	                        predicate.TypedGenerationChangedPredicate[*gpuv1.ClusterPolicy]{},
   353	                ),
   354	        )
   355	        if err != nil {
   356	                return err
   357	        }
   358	
   359	        nodePredicate := predicate.TypedFuncs[*corev1.Node]{
   360	                CreateFunc: func(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
   361	                        labels := e.Object.GetLabels()
   362	                        return hasGPULabels(labels)
   363	                },
   364	                UpdateFunc: func(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
   365	                        logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
   366	                        newLabels := e.ObjectNew.GetLabels()
   367	                        oldLabels := e.ObjectOld.GetLabels()
   368	                        nodeName := e.ObjectNew.GetName()
   369	
   370	                        needsUpdate := hasGPULabels(newLabels) && !maps.Equal(newLabels, oldLabels)
   371	
   372	                        if needsUpdate {
   373	                                logger.Info("Node labels have been changed",
   374	                                        "name", nodeName,
   375	                                )
   376	                        }
   377	                        return needsUpdate
   378	                },
   379	                DeleteFunc: func(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
   380	                        labels := e.Object.GetLabels()
   381	                        return hasGPULabels(labels)
   382	                },
   383	        }
   384	
   385	        // Watch for changes to node labels
   386	        err = c.Watch(
   387	                source.Kind(mgr.GetCache(),
   388	                        &corev1.Node{},
   389	                        handler.TypedEnqueueRequestsFromMapFunc[*corev1.Node](nodeMapFn),
   390	                        nodePredicate,
   391	                ),
   392	        )
   393	        if err != nil {
   394	                return err
   395	        }
   396	
   397	        // Watch for changes to secondary resources which each state manager manages
   398	        watchSources := stateManager.GetWatchSources(mgr)
   399	        for _, watchSource := range watchSources {
   400	                err = c.Watch(
   401	                        watchSource,
   402	                )
   403	                if err != nil {
   404	                        return fmt.Errorf("error setting up Watch for source type %v: %w", watchSource, err)
   405	                }
   406	        }
   407	
   408	        // Add an index key which allows our reconciler to quickly look up DaemonSets owned by an NVIDIADriver instance
   409	        if err := mgr.GetFieldIndexer().IndexField(ctx, &appsv1.DaemonSet{}, consts.NVIDIADriverControllerIndexKey, func(rawObj client.Object) []string {
   410	                ds := rawObj.(*appsv1.DaemonSet)
   411	                owner := metav1.GetControllerOf(ds)
   412	                if owner == nil {
   413	                        return nil
   414	                }
   415	                if owner.APIVersion != nvidiav1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion.String() || owner.Kind != nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverCRDName {
   416	                        return nil
   417	                }
   418	                return []string{owner.Name}
   419	        }); err != nil {
   420	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to add index key: %w", err)
   421	        }
   422	
   423	        return nil
   424	}
   425

    30	// Validator provides interface to validate NVIDIADriver fields
    31	type Validator interface {
    32	        Validate(ctx context.Context, cr *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver) error
    33	}
    34	
    35	// nodeSelectorValidator validates against the nodeSelector
    36	type nodeSelectorValidator struct {
    37	        client client.Client
    38	}
    39	
    40	// NewNodeSelectorValidator returns a new instance of nodeselector validator
    41	func NewNodeSelectorValidator(c client.Client) Validator {
    42	        return &nodeSelectorValidator{client: c}
    43	}
    44	
    45	// Check returns error when nodes matching with the selector labels of current instance of NVIDIADriver
    46	// are conflicting with other instances of NVIDIADriver
    47	func (nsv *nodeSelectorValidator) Validate(ctx context.Context, cr *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver) error {
    48	        drivers := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}
    49	        err := nsv.client.List(ctx, drivers)
    50	        if err != nil {
    51	                return err
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        names := map[string]struct{}{}
    55	        for di := range drivers.Items {
    56	                nodeList, err := nsv.getNVIDIADriverSelectedNodes(ctx, &drivers.Items[di])
    57	                if err != nil {
    58	                        return err
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                for ni := range nodeList.Items {
    62	                        if _, ok := names[nodeList.Items[ni].Name]; ok {
    63	                                return fmt.Errorf("conflicting NVIDIADriver NodeSelectors found for resource: %s, nodeSelector: %q", cr.Name, cr.Spec.NodeSelector)
    64	                        }
    65	
    66	                        names[nodeList.Items[ni].Name] = struct{}{}
    67	                }
    68	
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        return nil
    72	}
    73	
    74	// getNVIDIADriverSelectedNodes returns selected nodes based on the nodeselector labels set for a given NVIDIADriver instance
    75	func (nsv *nodeSelectorValidator) getNVIDIADriverSelectedNodes(ctx context.Context, cr *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver) (*corev1.NodeList, error) {
    76	        nodeList := &corev1.NodeList{}
    77	
    78	        if cr.Spec.NodeSelector == nil {
    79	                cr.Spec.NodeSelector = cr.GetNodeSelector()
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        selector := labels.Set(cr.Spec.NodeSelector).AsSelector()
    83	
    84	        opts := []client.ListOption{
    85	                client.MatchingLabelsSelector{Selector: selector},
    86	        }
    87	        err := nsv.client.List(ctx, nodeList, opts...)
    88	
    89	        return nodeList, err
    90	}

2026-05-29 23:08:56,800 - DEBUG - swea-lm-NVIDIA__gpu-operator-2258 - total_tokens_sent=25,986, total_tokens_received=311, total_cost=0.00, total_api_calls=5
2026-05-29 23:08:56,803 - INFO - swea-agent-NVIDIA__gpu-operator-2258 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the issue. Let me trace the flow:

1. When `NVIDIADriverReconciler.Reconcile` runs, it calls `r.nodeSelectorValidator.Validate(ctx, instance)` which checks for conflicts.
2. If there's a conflict (line 146-153), it sets state to NotReady and returns `reconcile.Result{}, nil` (no requeue, no error).
3. The problem is that when the conflicting CR (e.g., the default one) is deleted, the other CRs are NOT triggered for re-reconciliation.

Looking at the `SetupWithManager` function, I can see that:
- It watches NVIDIADriver with `predicate.TypedGenerationChangedPredicate` - which means only generation changes trigger reconciliation
- It doesn't watch for deletions of NVIDIADriver in a way that triggers other NVIDIADrivers

The fix should add a watch on NVIDIADriver resources that, when a NVIDIADriver is deleted (or updated), enqueues reconciliation for ALL other NVIDIADriver resources, similar to how ClusterPolicy changes trigger reconciliation of all NVIDIADrivers.

Let me look at the test file for the controller and validator to better understand:

   125	                },

   140	                },
   141	        }

   195	                                require.Contains(t, logs, tc.expectedLog)
   196	                        }

   198	        }

   201	func TestReconcileConflictSetsNotReadyState(t *testing.T) {
   202	        scheme := runtime.NewScheme()
   203	        require.NoError(t, nvidiav1alpha1.AddToScheme(scheme))
   204	        require.NoError(t, gpuv1.AddToScheme(scheme))
   205

   223	        }

   226	        updater := &FakeConditionUpdater{}
   227

   242	        }

   244	        _, err := reconciler.Reconcile(context.Background(), req)
   245	        require.NoError(t, err)
   246	        require.Equal(t, nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady, updater.LastErrorState)

2026-05-29 23:09:05,379 - INFO - swea-agent-NVIDIA__gpu-operator-2258 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a good understanding. Let me look at the controller to understand how watches work, particularly how ClusterPolicy changes trigger all NVIDIADriver reconciliations. The key issue is:

1. When a NVIDIADriver is deleted, other NVIDIADrivers should be re-reconciled to check if the conflict is resolved.
2. When a NVIDIADriver's spec (particularly nodeSelector) is updated, other NVIDIADrivers should also be re-reconciled.

Looking at the `SetupWithManager` function (lines 252-424), I can see:
- Line 282-290: Watches NVIDIADriver with `GenerationChangedPredicate` - only triggers on generation changes for the SAME object
- Line 347-357: Watches ClusterPolicy with a map function that enqueues ALL NVIDIADrivers
- Line 385-395: Watches Nodes with a map function that enqueues ALL NVIDIADrivers

The fix should add a watch on NVIDIADriver that, when any NVIDIADriver is created, updated, or deleted, enqueues reconciliation for ALL NVIDIADriver instances (similar to how ClusterPolicy and Node watches work).

Let me write a script to reproduce the issue

2026-05-29 23:10:22,220 - INFO - swea-agent-NVIDIA__gpu-operator-2258 - 💭 THOUGHT
Good. Now I understand the issue clearly. Let me look at the reconcile flow again:

In `SetupWithManager`, there are watches for:
1. NVIDIADriver with `GenerationChangedPredicate` - only watches for generation changes of the same CR
2. ClusterPolicy changes → enqueues all NVIDIADrivers
3. Node changes → enqueues all NVIDIADrivers

The missing watch is: **when a NVIDIADriver is created/deleted/updated, enqueue reconciliation for ALL other NVIDIADrivers** (or at least when deleted/updated since those can resolve conflicts).

Now, looking at the reconcile function, when there's a conflict (line 146-153), it returns `reconcile.Result{}, nil` - which means no requeue. This is intentionally not requeueing because the conflict won't resolve itself. But when the conflicting CR is deleted, nothing triggers the blocked CR to revalidate.

The fix should be to add a watch on NVIDIADriver that maps any NVIDIADriver event to reconciliation requests for all NVIDIADriver instances. This way, when one is deleted (or updated), all others get re-reconciled.

Let me implement this

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/controllers/nvidiadriver_controller.go   --old_str '// Watch for changes to secondary resources which each state manager manages
	watchSources := stateManager.GetWatchSources(mgr)
	for _, watchSource := range watchSources {
		err = c.Watch(
			watchSource,
		)
		if err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("error setting up Watch for source type %v: %w", watchSource, err)
		}
	}

	// Add an index key which allows our reconciler to quickly look up DaemonSets owned by an NVIDIADriver instance
	if err := mgr.GetFieldIndexer().IndexField(ctx, &appsv1.DaemonSet{}, consts.NVIDIADriverControllerIndexKey, func(rawObj client.Object) []string {
		ds := rawObj.(*appsv1.DaemonSet)
		owner := metav1.GetControllerOf(ds)
		if owner == nil {
			return nil
		}
		if owner.APIVersion != nvidiav1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion.String() || owner.Kind != nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverCRDName {
			return nil
		}
		return []string{owner.Name}
	}); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to add index key: %w", err)
	}

	return nil
}' --new_str '// Watch for changes to all NVIDIADriver instances. When any NVIDIADriver is
	// created, updated, or deleted, enqueue reconciliation for all NVIDIADriver
	// instances so they can revalidate nodeSelector conflicts.
	nvidiaDriverMapFn := func(ctx context.Context, nd *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver) []reconcile.Request {
		logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
		opts := []client.ListOption{}
		list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}

		err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
		if err != nil {
			logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
			return []reconcile.Request{}
		}

		reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
		for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
			reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
				reconcile.Request{
					NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
						Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
						Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
					},
				})
		}

		return reconcileRequests
	}

	err = c.Watch(
		source.Kind(
			mgr.GetCache(),
			&nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{},
			handler.TypedEnqueueRequestsFromMapFunc[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver](nvidiaDriverMapFn),
		),
	)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	// Watch for changes to secondary resources which each state manager manages
	watchSources := stateManager.GetWatchSources(mgr)
	for _, watchSource := range watchSources {
		err = c.Watch(
			watchSource,
		)
		if err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("error setting up Watch for source type %v: %w", watchSource, err)
		}
	}

	// Add an index key which allows our reconciler to quickly look up DaemonSets owned by an NVIDIADriver instance
	if err := mgr.GetFieldIndexer().IndexField(ctx, &appsv1.DaemonSet{}, consts.NVIDIADriverControllerIndexKey, func(rawObj client.Object) []string {
		ds := rawObj.(*appsv1.DaemonSet)
		owner := metav1.GetControllerOf(ds)
		if owner == nil {
			return nil
		}
		if owner.APIVersion != nvidiav1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion.String() || owner.Kind != nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverCRDName {
			return nil
		}
		return []string{owner.Name}
	}); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to add index key: %w", err)
	}

	return nil
}'

    55	        Scheme      *runtime.Scheme

    57	        Namespace   string

    64	//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=nvidia.com,resources=nvidiadrivers,verbs=get;list;watch;create;update;patch;delete
    65	//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=nvidia.com,resources=nvidiadrivers/status,verbs=get;update;patch

    68	// Reconcile is part of the main kubernetes reconciliation loop which aims to
    69	// move the current state of the cluster closer to the desired state.
    70	// TODO(user): Modify the Reconcile function to compare the state specified by
    71	// the NVIDIADriver object against the actual cluster state, and then
    72	// perform operations to make the cluster state reflect the state specified by
    73	// the user.
    74	//
    75	// For more details, check Reconcile and its Result here:
    76	// - https://pkg.go.dev/sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime@v0.8.3/pkg/reconcile
    77	func (r *NVIDIADriverReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
    78	        logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
    79	        logger.V(consts.LogLevelInfo).Info("Reconciling NVIDIADriver")
    80	
    81	        // Get the NvidiaDriver instance from this request
    82	        instance := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{}
    83	        if err := r.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, instance); err != nil {
    84	                if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
    85	                        // Request object not found, could have been deleted after reconcile request.
    86	                        // Owned objects are automatically garbage collected. For additional cleanup logic use finalizers.
    87	                        // Return and don't requeue
    88	                        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
    89	                }
    90	                wrappedErr := fmt.Errorf("error getting NVIDIADriver object: %w", err)
    91	                logger.Error(err, "error getting NVIDIADriver object")
    92	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
    93	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, wrappedErr.Error()); condErr != nil {
    94	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
    95	                }
    96	                // Error reading the object - requeue the request.
    97	                return reconcile.Result{}, wrappedErr
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        // Get the singleton NVIDIA ClusterPolicy object in the cluster.
   101	        clusterPolicyList := &gpuv1.ClusterPolicyList{}
   102	        if err := r.List(ctx, clusterPolicyList); err != nil {
   103	                wrappedErr := fmt.Errorf("error getting ClusterPolicy list: %w", err)
   104	                logger.Error(err, "error getting ClusterPolicy list")
   105	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   106	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   107	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   108	                }
   109	                return reconcile.Result{}, wrappedErr
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        if len(clusterPolicyList.Items) == 0 {
   113	                err := fmt.Errorf("no ClusterPolicy object found in the cluster")
   114	                logger.Error(err, "failed to get ClusterPolicy object")
   115	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   116	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   117	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   118	                }
   119	                return reconcile.Result{}, err
   120	        }
   121	        clusterPolicyInstance := clusterPolicyList.Items[0]
   122	
   123	        // Ensure that ClusterPolicy is configured to use NVIDIADriver CRD
   124	        if !clusterPolicyInstance.Spec.Driver.UseNvidiaDriverCRDType() {
   125	                msg := "useNvidiaDriverCRD is not enabled in ClusterPolicy"
   126	                logger.V(consts.LogLevelWarning).Info("NVIDIADriver reconciliation skipped", "reason", msg)
   127	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.Disabled
   128	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.Reconciled, msg); condErr != nil {
   129	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   130	                }
   131	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        // Create a new InfoCatalog which is a generic interface for passing information to state managers
   135	        infoCatalog := state.NewInfoCatalog()
   136	
   137	        // Add an entry for ClusterInfo, which was collected before the NVIDIADriver controller was started
   138	        infoCatalog.Add(state.InfoTypeClusterInfo, r.ClusterInfo)
   139	
   140	        // Add an entry for Clusterpolicy, which is needed to deploy the driver daemonset
   141	        infoCatalog.Add(state.InfoTypeClusterPolicyCR, clusterPolicyInstance)
   142	
   143	        // Verify the nodeSelector configured for this NVIDIADriver instance does
   144	        // not conflict with any other instances. This ensures only one driver
   145	        // is deployed per GPU node.
   146	        if err := r.nodeSelectorValidator.Validate(ctx, instance); err != nil {
   147	                logger.Error(err, "nodeSelector validation failed")
   148	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   149	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ConflictingNodeSelector, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   150	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   151	                }
   152	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        if instance.Spec.UsePrecompiledDrivers() && (instance.Spec.IsGDSEnabled() || instance.Spec.IsGDRCopyEnabled()) {
   156	                err := errors.New("GPUDirect Storage driver (nvidia-fs) and/or GDRCopy driver is not supported along with pre-compiled NVIDIA drivers")
   157	                logger.Error(err, "unsupported driver combination detected")
   158	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   159	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   160	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   161	                }
   162	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if instance.Spec.IsGDSEnabled() && instance.Spec.IsOpenKernelModulesRequired() && !instance.Spec.IsOpenKernelModulesEnabled() {
   166	                err := fmt.Errorf("GPUDirect Storage driver '%s' is only supported with NVIDIA OpenRM drivers. Please set 'useOpenKernelModules=true' to enable OpenRM mode", instance.Spec.GPUDirectStorage.Version)
   167	                logger.Error(err, "unsupported driver combination detected")
   168	                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
   169	                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   170	                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   171	                }
   172	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        // ensure that the specified K8s secret actually exists in the operator namespace
   176	        secretName := instance.Spec.SecretEnv
   177	        if len(secretName) > 0 {
   178	                key := client.ObjectKey{Namespace: r.Namespace, Name: secretName}
   179	                if err := r.Get(ctx, key, &corev1.Secret{}); err != nil {
   180	                        logger.Error(err, "failed to get secret")
   181	                        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
   182	                                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   183	                        }
   184	                        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   185	                }
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        // Sync state and update status
   189	        managerStatus := r.stateManager.SyncState(ctx, instance, infoCatalog)
   190	
   191	        // update CR status
   192	        if err := r.updateCrStatus(ctx, instance, managerStatus); err != nil {
   193	                return ctrl.Result{}, err
   194	        }
   195	
   196	        if managerStatus.Status != state.SyncStateReady {
   197	                logger.Info("NVIDIADriver instance is not ready")
   198	                var errorInfo error
   199	                for _, result := range managerStatus.StatesStatus {
   200	                        if result.Status != state.SyncStateReady && result.ErrInfo != nil {
   201	                                errorInfo = result.ErrInfo
   202	                                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, fmt.Sprintf("Error syncing state %s: %v", result.StateName, errorInfo.Error())); condErr != nil {
   203	                                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   204	                                }
   205	                                break
   206	                        }
   207	                }
   208	                // if no errors are reported from any state, then we would be waiting on driver daemonset pods
   209	                if errorInfo == nil {
   210	                        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.DriverNotReady, "Waiting for driver pod to be ready"); condErr != nil {
   211	                                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   212	                        }
   213	                }
   214	                return reconcile.Result{RequeueAfter: time.Second * 5}, nil
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsReady(ctx, instance, conditions.Reconciled, "All resources have been successfully reconciled"); condErr != nil {
   218	                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
   219	                return ctrl.Result{}, condErr
   220	        }
   221	        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   222	}
   223	
   224	func (r *NVIDIADriverReconciler) updateCrStatus(
   225	        ctx context.Context, cr *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver, status state.Results) error {
   226	        reqLogger := log.FromContext(ctx)
   227	
   228	        // Fetch latest instance and update state to avoid version mismatch
   229	        instance := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{}
   230	        err := r.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Name: cr.Name}, instance)
   231	        if err != nil {
   232	                reqLogger.Error(err, "Failed to get NVIDIADriver instance for status update")
   233	                return err
   234	        }
   235	
   236	        // Update global State
   237	        if instance.Status.State == nvidiav1alpha1.State(status.Status) {
   238	                return nil
   239	        }
   240	        instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.State(status.Status)
   241	
   242	        // send status update request to k8s API
   243	        reqLogger.V(consts.LogLevelInfo).Info("Updating CR Status", "Status", instance.Status)
   244	        err = r.Status().Update(ctx, instance)
   245	        if err != nil {
   246	                reqLogger.Error(err, "Failed to update CR status")
   247	                return err
   248	        }
   249	        return nil
   250	}

   252	// SetupWithManager sets up the controller with the Manager.
   253	func (r *NVIDIADriverReconciler) SetupWithManager(ctx context.Context, mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
   254	        // Create state manager
   255	        stateManager, err := state.NewManager(
   256	                nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverCRDName,
   257	                r.Namespace,
   258	                mgr.GetClient(),
   259	                mgr.GetScheme())
   260	        if err != nil {
   261	                return fmt.Errorf("error creating state manager: %v", err)
   262	        }
   263	        r.stateManager = stateManager
   264	
   265	        // initialize validators
   266	        r.nodeSelectorValidator = validator.NewNodeSelectorValidator(r.Client)
   267	
   268	        // initialize condition updater
   269	        r.conditionUpdater = conditions.NewNvDriverUpdater(mgr.GetClient())
   270	
   271	        // Create a new NVIDIADriver controller
   272	        c, err := controller.New("nvidia-driver-controller", mgr, controller.Options{
   273	                Reconciler:              r,
   274	                MaxConcurrentReconciles: 1,
   275	                RateLimiter:             workqueue.NewTypedItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter[reconcile.Request](minDelayCR, maxDelayCR),
   276	        })
   277	        if err != nil {
   278	                return err
   279	        }
   280	
   281	        // Watch for changes to the primary resource NVIDIaDriver
   282	        err = c.Watch(source.Kind(
   283	                mgr.GetCache(),
   284	                &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{},
   285	                &handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{},
   286	                predicate.TypedGenerationChangedPredicate[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{},
   287	        ),
   288	        )
   289	        if err != nil {
   290	                return err
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        // Watch for changes to ClusterPolicy. Whenever an event is generated for ClusterPolicy, enqueue
   294	        // a reconcile request for all NVIDIADriver instances.
   295	        mapFn := func(ctx context.Context, cp *gpuv1.ClusterPolicy) []reconcile.Request {
   296	                logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
   297	                opts := []client.ListOption{}
   298	                list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}
   299	
   300	                err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
   301	                if err != nil {
   302	                        logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
   303	                        return []reconcile.Request{}
   304	                }
   305	
   306	                reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
   307	                for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
   308	                        reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
   309	                                reconcile.Request{
   310	                                        NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
   311	                                                Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
   312	                                                Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
   313	                                        },
   314	                                })
   315	                }
   316	
   317	                return reconcileRequests
   318	        }
   319	
   320	        // Watch for changes to the Nodes. Whenever an event is generated for ClusterPolicy, enqueue
   321	        // a reconcile request for all NVIDIADr<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. 2026-05-29 23:12:08,714 - INFO - swea-agent-NVIDIA__gpu-operator-2258 - 💭 THOUGHT
All tests pass. Now let me also check if there's a similar issue with the `Reconcile` function returning `reconcile.Result{}, nil` on conflict validation - should it also requeue after some delay? Let me think about this...

Actually, looking at the PR description again: "custom CRs fail validation and exit reconcile without requeue." The issue is that when the default CR is deleted, the other CRs don't get reconciled. My fix adds a watch on NVIDIADriver resources so that when ANY NVIDIADriver is created/updated/deleted, ALL NVIDIADrivers get enqueued for reconciliation. This ensures that when the default CR is deleted, the other CRs will be re-reconciled.

However, I should also consider: should the reconcile function itself requeue on conflict? Currently it returns `reconcile.Result{}, nil` (no requeue). The idea is that the conflict won't resolve itself - but with my fix, when the other CR is deleted, it will trigger reconciliation. So the combination of:
1. Not requeueing on conflict (since it won't resolve by itself) 
2. But watching for other NVIDIADriver events to trigger re-reconciliation

...is correct.

But wait, there's another consideration: what if the conflict is due to the nodeSelector of the current CR being updated? In that case, the `GenerationChangedPredicate` on the first watch would trigger reconciliation for the SAME CR. But what if the conflict is between CR A and CR B, and CR B updates its nodeSelector? With my new watch, any change to CR B would trigger reconciliation of ALL CRs including CR A. That's correct.

Let me also think about edge cases:
1. **Creating a new NVIDIADriver**: The new watch will trigger reconciliation for all existing NVIDIADrivers. This is good because a new CR might conflict with existing ones.
2. **Deleting a NVIDIADriver**: The new watch will trigger reconciliation for all remaining NVIDIADrivers. This is exactly what the bug report asks for.
3. **Updating a NVIDIADriver's nodeSelector**: The new watch will trigger reconciliation for all NVIDIADrivers. This is good because the updated nodeSelector might resolve or create new conflicts.
4. **Updating a NVIDIADriver's status**: The new watch doesn't use a predicate filter, so it would also trigger on status updates. This could cause unnecessary reconciliation loops. Let me check if this is a problem...

Looking at the existing watch for NVIDIADriver (line 282-288), it uses `predicate.TypedGenerationChangedPredicate` which only triggers on spec changes (generation changes), not status updates. But my new watch doesn't have a predicate, so it would also trigger on status updates.

However, looking at the map functions for ClusterPolicy and Nodes, they also don't filter by generation - they just map any event to all NVIDIADrivers. So my approach is consistent with the existing pattern.

But there's a potential infinite loop: when a NVIDIADriver is reconciled, it updates its status. The status update triggers the watch, which enqueues all NVIDIADrivers again. However, this is the same pattern used for ClusterPolicy and Nodes, and it seems to work because the reconcile function is idempotent - when it finds the state is already correct, it returns early (line 237-239 `updateCrStatus` returns nil if state hasn't changed).

Let me verify that the reconciliation is indeed idempotent. Looking at `updateCrStatus`:
- Line 237-239: If `instance.Status.State == status.Status`, return nil (no update needed)
- But the status update itself would trigger the watch again... though actually, the status update is done via `r.Status().Update(ctx, instance)` which updates the status subresource. In Kubernetes, status updates don't increment the generation metadata field.

The first watch (line 282-288) uses `GenerationChangedPredicate` which filters out status updates. But my new watch doesn't have this filter. So status updates WOULD trigger the new watch, causing all NVIDIADrivers to be re-reconciled. This could lead to a reconciliation loop.

Let me add a predicate to the new watch to only react to actual spec changes (generation changes) and deletions, but not status updates. Actually, we need to also react to deletions (which don't have generation changes). Let me think about this more carefully...

Actually, looking at the problem from the perspective of the PR description: the issue is that when a conflicting NVIDIADriver is DELETED, other NVIDIADrivers don't get re-reconciled. So we need the watch to fire on DELETE events. 

But if we add a `GenerationChangedPredicate`, it would filter out both status updates AND delete events (since delete events don't have a generation change - the old object is just removed).

Let me look at what events we need:
1. **Create**: A new NVIDIADriver might conflict with existing ones → should trigger re-reconciliation of all
2. **Update with spec change**: nodeSelector changes could resolve/create conflicts → should trigger re-reconciliation
3. **Delete**: Conflicting CR removed → should trigger re-reconciliation
4. **Update with status only**: Should NOT trigger re-reconciliation (to avoid infinite loops)

So I need a custom predicate that allows create, delete, and spec-change updates, but filters out status-only updates.

Let me update my implementation:



🎬 ACTION

			logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")

						Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
						Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
					},
				})

		logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
		opts := []client.ListOption{}
		list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}

		err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
		if err != nil {
			logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
			return []reconcile.Request{}
		}

		reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
		for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
			reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
				reconcile.Request{
					NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
						Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
						Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
					},
				})
		}

		return reconcileRequests
	}

	// Use a predicate that triggers on create, delete, and spec changes (generation changes),
	// but filters out status-only updates to avoid infinite reconciliation loops.
	nvidiaDriverPredicate := predicate.TypedFuncs[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{
		CreateFunc: func(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]) bool {
			return true
		},
		UpdateFunc: func(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]) bool {
			// Only trigger on generation changes (spec changes), not status updates
			return e.ObjectNew.GetGeneration() != e.ObjectOld.GetGeneration()
		},
		DeleteFunc: func(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]) bool {
			return true
		},
	}

	err = c.Watch(
		source.Kind(
			mgr.GetCache(),
			&nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{},
			handler.TypedEnqueueRequestsFromMapFunc[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver](nvidiaDriverMapFn),
			nvidiaDriverPredicate,
		),
	)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}'

2026-05-29 23:13:14,998 - INFO - swea-agent-NVIDIA__gpu-operator-2258 - 💭 THOUGHT
The change looks good. Let me now think about edge cases:

1. **Delete event**: When a NVIDIADriver is deleted, `DeleteFunc` returns `true`, which triggers the map function. The map function lists all remaining NVIDIADrivers and enqueues them for reconciliation. This is exactly what we need.

2. **Create event**: When a new NVIDIADriver is created, `CreateFunc` returns `true`, which triggers reconciliation of all existing NVIDIADrivers. This ensures new conflicts are detected immediately.

3. **Update event (spec change)**: When a NVIDIADriver's spec changes (e.g., nodeSelector is updated), `UpdateFunc` checks generation change and returns `true` only if the spec actually changed. This triggers reconciliation of all NVIDIADrivers, ensuring conflicts are re-evaluated.

4. **Update event (status only)**: `UpdateFunc` returns `false` because the generation doesn't change on status updates. This prevents infinite reconciliation loops.

5. **The existing watch on line 282-288** still exists and handles the case where a CR's own spec changes (triggering its own reconciliation). The new watch complements this by ensuring OTHER CRs are also reconciled when any CR changes.

Let me also check that there's no issue with the "delete" case - when a NVIDIADriver is deleted, we enqueue reconciliation for all NVIDIADrivers. The reconcile function for a deleted CR would just return early (line 84-88) because `IsNotFound` would be true. But for the OTHER CRs, the reconcile would proceed and re-validate. This is correct behavior.

One more thing to consider: the `nvidiaDriverMapFn` lists all NVIDIADrivers including the one that triggered the event. But that's fine because:
- For the triggering CR itself, the first watch (line 282) already handles its own reconciliation
- The extra reconciliation is harmless (idempotent)

I'm satisfied with the fix. Let me do a final build and test to make sure everything is clean:

+        // Get the NvidiaDriver instance from this request
+        instance := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{}
+        if err := r.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, instance); err != nil {
+                if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+                        // Request object not found, could have been deleted after reconcile request.
+                        // Owned objects are automatically garbage collected. For additional cleanup logic use finalizers.
+                        // Return and don't requeue
+                        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
+                }
+                wrappedErr := fmt.Errorf("error getting NVIDIADriver object: %w", err)
+                logger.Error(err, "error getting NVIDIADriver object")
+                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
+                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, wrappedErr.Error()); condErr != nil {
+                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                }
+                // Error reading the object - requeue the request.
+                return reconcile.Result{}, wrappedErr
+        }
+
+        // Get the singleton NVIDIA ClusterPolicy object in the cluster.
+        clusterPolicyList := &gpuv1.ClusterPolicyList{}
+        if err := r.List(ctx, clusterPolicyList); err != nil {
+                wrappedErr := fmt.Errorf("error getting ClusterPolicy list: %w", err)
+                logger.Error(err, "error getting ClusterPolicy list")
+                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
+                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
+                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                }
+                return reconcile.Result{}, wrappedErr
+        }
+
+        if len(clusterPolicyList.Items) == 0 {
+                err := fmt.Errorf("no ClusterPolicy object found in the cluster")
+                logger.Error(err, "failed to get ClusterPolicy object")
+                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
+                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
+                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                }
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+        clusterPolicyInstance := clusterPolicyList.Items[0]
+
+        // Ensure that ClusterPolicy is configured to use NVIDIADriver CRD
+        if !clusterPolicyInstance.Spec.Driver.UseNvidiaDriverCRDType() {
+                msg := "useNvidiaDriverCRD is not enabled in ClusterPolicy"
+                logger.V(consts.LogLevelWarning).Info("NVIDIADriver reconciliation skipped", "reason", msg)
+                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.Disabled
+                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.Reconciled, msg); condErr != nil {
+                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                }
+                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
+        }
+
+        // Create a new InfoCatalog which is a generic interface for passing information to state managers
+        infoCatalog := state.NewInfoCatalog()
+
+        // Add an entry for ClusterInfo, which was collected before the NVIDIADriver controller was started
+        infoCatalog.Add(state.InfoTypeClusterInfo, r.ClusterInfo)
+
+        // Add an entry for Clusterpolicy, which is needed to deploy the driver daemonset
+        infoCatalog.Add(state.InfoTypeClusterPolicyCR, clusterPolicyInstance)
+
+        // Verify the nodeSelector configured for this NVIDIADriver instance does
+        // not conflict with any other instances. This ensures only one driver
+        // is deployed per GPU node.
+        if err := r.nodeSelectorValidator.Validate(ctx, instance); err != nil {
+                logger.Error(err, "nodeSelector validation failed")
+                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
+                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ConflictingNodeSelector, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
+                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                }
+                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
+        }
+
+        if instance.Spec.UsePrecompiledDrivers() && (instance.Spec.IsGDSEnabled() || instance.Spec.IsGDRCopyEnabled()) {
+                err := errors.New("GPUDirect Storage driver (nvidia-fs) and/or GDRCopy driver is not supported along with pre-compiled NVIDIA drivers")
+                logger.Error(err, "unsupported driver combination detected")
+                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
+                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
+                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                }
+                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
+        }
+
+        if instance.Spec.IsGDSEnabled() && instance.Spec.IsOpenKernelModulesRequired() && !instance.Spec.IsOpenKernelModulesEnabled() {
+                err := fmt.Errorf("GPUDirect Storage driver '%s' is only supported with NVIDIA OpenRM drivers. Please set 'useOpenKernelModules=true' to enable OpenRM mode", instance.Spec.GPUDirectStorage.Version)
+                logger.Error(err, "unsupported driver combination detected")
+                instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.NotReady
+                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
+                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                }
+                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
+        }
+
+        // ensure that the specified K8s secret actually exists in the operator namespace
+        secretName := instance.Spec.SecretEnv
+        if len(secretName) > 0 {
+                key := client.ObjectKey{Namespace: r.Namespace, Name: secretName}
+                if err := r.Get(ctx, key, &corev1.Secret{}); err != nil {
+                        logger.Error(err, "failed to get secret")
+                        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, err.Error()); condErr != nil {
+                                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                        }
+                        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Sync state and update status
+        managerStatus := r.stateManager.SyncState(ctx, instance, infoCatalog)
+
+        // update CR status
+        if err := r.updateCrStatus(ctx, instance, managerStatus); err != nil {
+                return ctrl.Result{}, err
+        }
+
+        if managerStatus.Status != state.SyncStateReady {
+                logger.Info("NVIDIADriver instance is not ready")
+                var errorInfo error
+                for _, result := range managerStatus.StatesStatus {
+                        if result.Status != state.SyncStateReady && result.ErrInfo != nil {
+                                errorInfo = result.ErrInfo
+                                if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.ReconcileFailed, fmt.Sprintf("Error syncing state %s: %v", result.StateName, errorInfo.Error())); condErr != nil {
+                                        logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                                }
+                                break
+                        }
+                }
+                // if no errors are reported from any state, then we would be waiting on driver daemonset pods
+                if errorInfo == nil {
+                        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsError(ctx, instance, conditions.DriverNotReady, "Waiting for driver pod to be ready"); condErr != nil {
+                                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                        }
+                }
+                return reconcile.Result{RequeueAfter: time.Second * 5}, nil
+        }
+
+        if condErr := r.conditionUpdater.SetConditionsReady(ctx, instance, conditions.Reconciled, "All resources have been successfully reconciled"); condErr != nil {
+                logger.Error(condErr, "failed to set condition")
+                return ctrl.Result{}, condErr
+        }
+        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
 }

-	// send status update request to k8s API
-	reqLogger.V(consts.LogLevelInfo).Info("Updating CR Status", "Status", instance.Status)
-	err = r.Status().Update(ctx, instance)
-	if err != nil {
-		reqLogger.Error(err, "Failed to update CR status")
-		return err
-	}
-	return nil
+        ctx context.Context, cr *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver, status state.Results) error {
+        reqLogger := log.FromContext(ctx)
+
+        // Fetch latest instance and update state to avoid version mismatch
+        instance := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{}
+        err := r.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Name: cr.Name}, instance)
+        if err != nil {
+                reqLogger.Error(err, "Failed to get NVIDIADriver instance for status update")
+                return err
+        }
+
+        // Update global State
+        if instance.Status.State == nvidiav1alpha1.State(status.Status) {
+                return nil
+        }
+        instance.Status.State = nvidiav1alpha1.State(status.Status)
+
+        // send status update request to k8s API
+        reqLogger.V(consts.LogLevelInfo).Info("Updating CR Status", "Status", instance.Status)
+        err = r.Status().Update(ctx, instance)
+        if err != nil {
+                reqLogger.Error(err, "Failed to update CR status")
+                return err
+        }
+        return nil
 }

+        // initialize validators
+        r.nodeSelectorValidator = validator.NewNodeSelectorValidator(r.Client)
+
+        // initialize condition updater
+        r.conditionUpdater = conditions.NewNvDriverUpdater(mgr.GetClient())
+
+        // Create a new NVIDIADriver controller
+        c, err := controller.New("nvidia-driver-controller", mgr, controller.Options{
+                Reconciler:              r,
+                MaxConcurrentReconciles: 1,
+                RateLimiter:             workqueue.NewTypedItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter[reconcile.Request](minDelayCR, maxDelayCR),
+        })
+        if err != nil {

+                mgr.GetCache(),
+                &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{},
+                &handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{},
+                predicate.TypedGenerationChangedPredicate[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{},
+        ),
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+
+        // Watch for changes to ClusterPolicy. Whenever an event is generated for ClusterPolicy, enqueue
+        // a reconcile request for all NVIDIADriver instances.
+        mapFn := func(ctx context.Context, cp *gpuv1.ClusterPolicy) []reconcile.Request {
+                logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
+                opts := []client.ListOption{}
+                list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}
+
+                err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
+                if err != nil {
+                        logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
+                        return []reconcile.Request{}
+                }
+
+                reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
+                for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
+                        reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
+                                reconcile.Request{
+                                        NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
+                                                Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
+                                                Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
+                                        },
+                                })
+                }
+
+                return reconcileRequests
+        }
+
+        // Watch for changes to the Nodes. Whenever an event is generated for ClusterPolicy, enqueue
+        // a reconcile request for all NVIDIADriver instances.
+        nodeMapFn := func(ctx context.Context, cp *corev1.Node) []reconcile.Request {
+                logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
+                opts := []client.ListOption{}
+                list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}
+
+                err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
+                if err != nil {
+                        logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
+                        return []reconcile.Request{}
+                }
+
+                reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
+                for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
+                        reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
+                                reconcile.Request{
+                                        NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
+                                                Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
+                                                Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
+                                        },
+                                })
+                }
+
+                return reconcileRequests
+        }
+
+        err = c.Watch(
+                source.Kind(
+                        mgr.GetCache(),
+                        &gpuv1.ClusterPolicy{},
+                        handler.TypedEnqueueRequestsFromMapFunc[*gpuv1.ClusterPolicy](mapFn),
+                        predicate.TypedGenerationChangedPredicate[*gpuv1.ClusterPolicy]{},
+                ),
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+
+        nodePredicate := predicate.TypedFuncs[*corev1.Node]{
+                CreateFunc: func(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+                        labels := e.Object.GetLabels()
+                        return hasGPULabels(labels)
+                },
+                UpdateFunc: func(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+                        logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
+                        newLabels := e.ObjectNew.GetLabels()
+                        oldLabels := e.ObjectOld.GetLabels()
+                        nodeName := e.ObjectNew.GetName()
+
+                        needsUpdate := hasGPULabels(newLabels) && !maps.Equal(newLabels, oldLabels)
+
+                        if needsUpdate {
+                                logger.Info("Node labels have been changed",
+                                        "name", nodeName,
+                                )
+                        }
+                        return needsUpdate
+                },
+                DeleteFunc: func(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+                        labels := e.Object.GetLabels()
+                        return hasGPULabels(labels)
+                },
+        }
+
+        // Watch for changes to node labels
+        err = c.Watch(
+                source.Kind(mgr.GetCache(),
+                        &corev1.Node{},
+                        handler.TypedEnqueueRequestsFromMapFunc[*corev1.Node](nodeMapFn),
+                        nodePredicate,
+                ),
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+
+        // Watch for changes to all NVIDIADriver instances. When any NVIDIADriver is
+        // created, updated, or deleted, enqueue reconciliation for all NVIDIADriver
+        // instances so they can revalidate nodeSelector conflicts.
+        nvidiaDriverMapFn := func(ctx context.Context, nd *nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver) []reconcile.Request {
+                logger := log.FromContext(ctx)
+                opts := []client.ListOption{}
+                list := &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverList{}
+
+                err := mgr.GetClient().List(ctx, list, opts...)
+                if err != nil {
+                        logger.Error(err, "Unable to list NVIDIADriver resources")
+                        return []reconcile.Request{}
+                }
+
+                reconcileRequests := []reconcile.Request{}
+                for _, nvidiaDriver := range list.Items {
+                        reconcileRequests = append(reconcileRequests,
+                                reconcile.Request{
+                                        NamespacedName: types.NamespacedName{
+                                                Name:      nvidiaDriver.GetName(),
+                                                Namespace: nvidiaDriver.GetNamespace(),
+                                        },
+                                })
+                }
+
+                return reconcileRequests
+        }
+
+        // Use a predicate that triggers on create, delete, and spec changes (generation changes),
+        // but filters out status-only updates to avoid infinite reconciliation loops.
+        nvidiaDriverPredicate := predicate.TypedFuncs[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]{
+                CreateFunc: func(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]) bool {
+                        return true
+                },
+                UpdateFunc: func(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]) bool {
+                        // Only trigger on generation changes (spec changes), not status updates
+                        return e.ObjectNew.GetGeneration() != e.ObjectOld.GetGeneration()
+                },
+                DeleteFunc: func(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver]) bool {
+                        return true
+                },
+        }
+
+        err = c.Watch(
+                source.Kind(
+                        mgr.GetCache(),
+                        &nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver{},
+                        handler.TypedEnqueueRequestsFromMapFunc[*nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriver](nvidiaDriverMapFn),
+                        nvidiaDriverPredicate,
+                ),
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+
+        // Watch for changes to secondary resources which each state manager manages
+        watchSources := stateManager.GetWatchSources(mgr)
+        for _, watchSource := range watchSources {
+                err = c.Watch(
+                        watchSource,
+                )
+                if err != nil {
+                        return fmt.Errorf("error setting up Watch for source type %v: %w", watchSource, err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Add an index key which allows our reconciler to quickly look up DaemonSets owned by an NVIDIADriver instance
+        if err := mgr.GetFieldIndexer().IndexField(ctx, &appsv1.DaemonSet{}, consts.NVIDIADriverControllerIndexKey, func(rawObj client.Object) []string {
+                ds := rawObj.(*appsv1.DaemonSet)
+                owner := metav1.GetControllerOf(ds)
+                if owner == nil {
+                        return nil
+                }
+                if owner.APIVersion != nvidiav1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion.String() || owner.Kind != nvidiav1alpha1.NVIDIADriverCRDName {
+                        return nil
+                }
+                return []string{owner.Name}
+        }); err != nil {
+                return fmt.Errorf("failed to add index key: %w", err)
+        }
+
+        return nil
 }
